of the Grafana v38 schema migration bug:\\n\\n## Files and Functions\\n\\n### 1. Schema version registration: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`\\nThe `GetMigrations` function registers the V38 migration in a map keyed by schema version integer 38. The constant `LATEST_VERSION = 42` is defined here. This is where V38 is registered and becomes part of the migration pipeline.\\n\\n### 2. V38 migration implementation: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go`\\nThe entry point is `V38(ctx, dashboard)`, which calls `processPanelsV38(panels)`. The function `processPanelsV38` iterates over all panels (including nested panels within row panels) and migrates table panels from the old `displayMode` string format to the structured `cellOptions` object format.\\n\\n**The flawed conditional** that causes fieldConfig override loss when `defaults.custom` is absent:\\n\\nIn the buggy version of the code, `migrateOverrides(fieldConfig)` would have been placed *inside* the nested conditional block:\\n\\n```go\\nif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n    if custom, ok := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n        // defaults migration ...\\n        migrateOverrides(fieldConfig)  // BUG: only called when custom exists\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThis means that for table panels where `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` is absent (panels relying only on field override rules for column widths and display alignment), the `migrateOverrides` call is never reached. Field overrides containing `custom.displayMode` properties are never migrated to `custom.cellOptions`, so the table panel silently loses its cell display configuration after the v38 migration.\\n\\nThe current code shows the fix with an explicit comment at line 130:\\n```go\\n// Update any overrides referencing the cell display mode\\n// This must be called regardless of whether defaults.custom exists\\nmigrateOverrides(fieldConfig)\\n```\\n\\nThe `migrateOverrides` function iterates over `fieldConfig.overrides`, finds properties with `id == \\\"custom.displayMode\\\"`, and rewrites them as `id = \\\"custom.cellOptions\\\"` with a structured value. Without this call, column alignment/display overrides are left as the now-unrecognized `custom.displayMode` key, causing the Grafana table panel renderer to ignore them.\\n\\n### 3. TypeScript counterpart: `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`\\nThe TypeScript frontend migrator also implements the v38 migration at line 644 (inside `updateSchema`). It uses the conditional:\\n```typescript\\nconst displayMode = panel.fieldConfig.defaults?.custom?.displayMode;\\nif (displayMode !== undefined) { /* migrate defaults */ }\\nif (panel.fieldConfig?.overrides) { /* migrate overrides */ }\\n```\\nHere the overrides branch is correctly placed outside the `displayMode` check. The `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION` constant is set to 42 (latest).\\n\\n## Summary\\n- **Schema version constant file**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go` — `GetMigrations()` registers `38: V38`.\\n- **Migration function with the bug**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go` — `processPanelsV38` function; the flawed conditional is the nested `if custom, ok := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok` guard that caused `migrateOverrides` to be skipped when `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` was absent.\\n- **TypeScript version**: `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts` — anonymous panel upgrade function at oldVersion < 38 block.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
